$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / While_Loops_Printing1

::While Loops Level 1 #000::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>int d = 82;
while (d > 42)
\{
	cout << d << " ";
	d -= 10;
\}	{
	=82 72 62 52 
	~72 62 52 
	~72 62 52 42 
	~82 72 62 
	~82 72 62 52 42 
	}

::While Loops Level 1 #001::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>int h = 3;
while (h <= 7)
\{
	cout << h << " ";
	h += 1;
\}	{
	=3 4 5 6 7 
	~4 5 6 7 
	~4 5 6 7 8 
	~3 4 5 6 
	~3 4 5 6 7 8 
	}

while (j > 72)
\{
	cout << j << " ";
	j -= 10;
\}	{
	=95 85 75 
	~85 75 
	~85 75 65 
	~95 85 
	~95 85 75 65 
	}

<pre>int h = 10000;
while (h >= 1)
\{
	cout << h << " ";
	h /= 10;
\}	{
	=10000 1000 100 10 1 
	~1000 100 10 1 
	~1000 100 10 1 0 
	~10000 1000 100 10 
	~10000 1000 100 10 1 0 
	}

::While Loops Level 3 #500::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>int i = 5;
while (i >= 3)
\{
	int j= 7;
	while (j < 10)
	\{
		cout << '*' << endl;
		j += 1;
	\}
\}</pre>	{
	=9
	~4
	~3
	~12
	~16
	}

<pre>int i = 4;
while (i <= 227)
\{
	int j= 1;

	\{
		cout << '*' << endl;
		j *= 10;
	\}
\}</pre>	{
	=6
	~3
	~2
	~5
	~9
	}

<pre>int i = 2;
while (i < 32)
\{
	int j= 3;
	while (j <= 12)
	\{
		cout << '*' << endl;
		j *= 2;
	\}
\}</pre>	{
	=6
	~3
	~2
	~7
	~9
	}
